            ALLPLAYERS = json.load(f)

        if(player['Large_Damage'] < damage):
            ALLPLAYERS[member.id]['Large_Damage'] = damage
        with open('Players.json', 'w') as f:
            json.dump(ALLPLAYERS, f)```
11 Jan 2017 02:26:32 : Pokemon Mystery Dungeon, general, Wertfuzzy77#0274, to ```py
    async def dealDamage(self, member, damage):
        with open('Players.json', 'r') as f:
            ALLPLAYERS = json.load(f)
        try:
            player = await self.checkLevel(ALLPLAYERS[member.id])
        except:
            print("NEW PLAYER: {}".format(ctx.message.author.name))
            ALLPLAYERS[member.id] = {"Name" : member.name, "Level": 0, "XP": 0, "Large_Damage" : 0, "Takedowns" : 0}    
            player = ALLPLAYERS[member.id]
        if(player['Large_Damage'] < damage):
            ALLPLAYERS[member.id]['Large_Damage'] = damage
        with open('Players.json', 'w') as f:
            json.dump(ALLPLAYERS, f)```

        result = random.choice(self.books)
        return result

import random

class Spinner:

    def __init__(self, books):
        self.books = books

    def spin(self):
        result = random.choice(self.books)
        return result

def super_spin(num_times):
    for _ in range(num_times):
        common_books = Spinner(['Gust Arcana', 'Shield Arcana', 'Needle Arcana', 'Hardy Vine Arcana', 'Tortoiseshell Arcana'])
        uncommon_books = Spinner(['Fireball Arcana', 'Molten Iron Arcana', 'Feather Arcana', 'Katana Arcana', 'Hurricane Arcana', 'Waterfall Arcana'])
        rare_books = Spinner(['Void Arcana', 'Gold Arcana', 'Cascade Arcana', 'Sunlight Arcana', 'Diamond Arcana'])
        result = random.randrange(200)
        print(result)
        if result < 1:
            print("Phoenix Arcana - Rare Find!")
        elif result < 11:
            print(rare_books.spin() + " - Rare Find!")
        elif result < 36:
            print(uncommon_books.spin() + " - Uncommon Find!")
        else:
            print(common_books.spin())

super_spin(6)
```
